I have been using the small bubble glass attachment and found that it causes my skin to dry out and peel. Then I place the end of the tube on any acne spot and release my finger, holding it in place for about 10 seconds. I then put my finger back on the tube and lift the tube away from my skin. That keeps it from arcing (sparking) and I find that works much better for me. When I do a treatment like that, the spot is gone within a day or so. I only have time to use it once a day (usually in the morning before I get ready for work). Make sure your skin is very clean and sterilize the glass tubes with an antibacterial wipe or rubbing alcohol. Use a dry paper towel or clean cloth to handle the tubes.   198. My comments after reading the reviews and using it myself for three weeks.<br /><br />Read about a process called Thermage to understand that the benefits are not intended to be seen immediately. I had a few Thermage treatment in a doctor's office, very expensive and painful, where it was explained to me that it TAKES TIME for the underlying collagen to regenerate. You may not see any reversal of aging, but more likely the reduction of aging by building the collagen beneath. The Thermage treatment places the wand directly on the skin to penetrate the underlying layers, which is how you should be using this machine, and moving the wand slowly over the trouble areas to allow the heat to penetrate. If you lift it, not only will you get that painful snapping effect, but you're sending the heat onto the skin, not into it as you should.<br /><br />As for its safety and operation, you can no more electrocute yourself with it than you can with any other electrical appliance--just be sensible and don't throw it in the bathtub. Mine came beautifully boxed, all intact, and seems to operate as it should--no reduction or fluctuation in power. My only caution is the fragility of the wands, so since I prefer the mushroom, I leave it in the machine and store it carefully in a spare drawer. I also recommend NOT touching the stem of the wand while it's operating, not because it will hurt you, but it's a little startling and may cause you to drop the wand. Since the proper amount of time has not yet passed to see how effective this is in comparison with the full-fledged Thermage, I can only give it four stars.

Second, there are LOTS of websites available that teach you what HF is, what it's good for and how to use each individual electrode. There are also countless videos on YouTube that offer advice and demonstrations. If you've never used HF before and have no idea how to use it, WATCH THESE VIDEOS FIRST! Arm yourself with knowledge before using any machine you are unfamiliar with! Third, HF creates ozone and has antibacterial properties. You should use it on CLEAN skin. If you choose to use it with a moisturizer of some sort, make sure it is alcohol-free. Also, do not use alcohol to clean your electrodes. Wipe the glass part ONLY with mild cleanser and water. Fifth, this machine is not intended to stimulate muscles, therefore, you will not feel 'twitching' or 'jumping' light you might with other machines.
